	<div class="entry-content-wrap">
		
<div class="entry-content single-content">
	
<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column506_bd3237-9e"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col"><div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id506_78c559-f3 alignnone wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-1-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-top">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading" style="font-size:28px">Hello! I&#8217;m Katarina, the creator of Adventour Begins!</h2>

<p class="kt-adv-heading506_684ea8-5f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading506_684ea8-5f">On my blog, you’ll find guides to 150+ cruise destinations, travel tips, packing advice, and insights into cruise ship jobs and life onboard. </p>
